    <script>
      document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () {
        const container = document.getElementById("items-container");
        const prevBtn = document.getElementById("prev");
        const nextBtn = document.getElementById("next");
        const itemWidth = 160;
        const items = Array.from(container.children);
        const itemsCount = items.length;
        let currentIndex = 0;
        let isTransitioning = false;
        const clonesStart = [];
        const clonesEnd = [];
        for (let i = 0; i < itemsCount; i++) {
          const clone = items[i].cloneNode(true);
          clone.setAttribute("data-clone", "end");
          clonesEnd.push(clone);
          container.appendChild(clone);
        }
        for (let i = 0; i < itemsCount; i++) {
          const clone = items[i].cloneNode(true);
          clone.setAttribute("data-clone", "start");
          clonesStart.push(clone);
          container.insertBefore(clone, items[0]);
        }
        const initialPosition = -itemsCount * itemWidth;
        container.style.transform = `translateX(${initialPosition}px)`;
        function next() {
          if (isTransitioning) return;
          isTransitioning = true;
          currentIndex++;
          const newPosition = initialPosition - currentIndex * itemWidth;
          container.style.transition = "transform 0.5s ease";
          container.style.transform = `translateX(${newPosition}px)`;
          if (currentIndex >= itemsCount) {
            setTimeout(() => {
              isTransitioning = false;
              currentIndex = 0;
              container.style.transition = "none";
              container.style.transform = `translateX(${initialPosition}px)`;
            }, 500);
          } else {
            setTimeout(() => {
              isTransitioning = false;
            }, 500);
          }
        }
        function prev() {
          if (isTransitioning) return;
          isTransitioning = true;
          if (currentIndex <= 0) {
            currentIndex = itemsCount;
            container.style.transition = "none";
            container.style.transform = `translateX(${
              initialPosition - itemsCount * itemWidth
            }px)`;
            container.offsetHeight;
            setTimeout(() => {
              container.style.transition = "transform 0.5s ease";
              currentIndex--;
              const newPosition = initialPosition - currentIndex * itemWidth;
              container.style.transform = `translateX(${newPosition}px)`;
              setTimeout(() => {
                isTransitioning = false;
              }, 500);
            }, 50);
          } else {
            currentIndex--;
            const newPosition = initialPosition - currentIndex * itemWidth;
            container.style.transition = "transform 0.5s ease";
            container.style.transform = `translateX(${newPosition}px)`;
            setTimeout(() => {
              isTransitioning = false;
            }, 500);
          }
        }
        nextBtn.addEventListener("click", next);
        prevBtn.addEventListener("click", prev);
      });
    </script></div>
</div></div></section><section class="o-section o-board--K o-board--K-v2"><div class="o-container o-container--title"></div><div class="o-container o-container--board o-container--row-1"><div class="u-grid u-grid-columns-3"><div class="u-grid-col-span-2 u-flex"><div allow class="o-container--module u-flex u-flex-grow-shrink"><article class="c-article c-article--big"><span class="labelIcon"></span><figure class="c-article__thumb"><a title="España recibirá otros 166 millones de fondos europeos para reparar los daños por la DANA" href="/nacional/espana-recibira-otros-166-millones-fondos-europeos-para-reparar-danos-causados-por-dana-valencia_6537322_0.html"><picture><!----><source media="(min-width: 768px)" width="640" height="360" srcset="https://imagenes.20minutos.es/files/image_640_360/uploads/imagenes/2024/12/01/fotografo-jorge-paris-hernandez-previsiones-20m-tema-especial-dana-valencia-paiporta-11.jpeg"><source media="(min-width: 480px)" width="990" height="556" srcset="https://imagenes.20minutos.es/files/image_990_556/uploads/imagenes/2024/12/01/fotografo-jorge-paris-hernandez-previsiones-20m-tema-especial-dana-valencia-paiporta-11.jpeg"><img loading="lazy" alt="fotografo: Jorge Paris Hernandez[[[PREVISIONES 20M]]] tema: Especial Dana Valencia.
